【2020년 군사교육 본인선택 실시 안내】

2020년 전문연구/산업기능요원 군사교육소집일자 본인선택을 2020년 1월 22일(수) 14:00부터 공석 마감 시까지 병무청 홈페이지에서 접수합니다.

본인선택 대상은 전문연구/산업기능요원 편입 후 1년 미만인 사람(편입일 기준, 군사교육소집일자까지 1년 미만인 사람)이며,

「병무청 홈페이지 ⇒ 병무민원포털 ⇒ 전문/산업 ⇒ 전문연구/산업기능/승선 민원신청 ⇒ 전문연구/산업기능요원 군사교육소집일자 본인선택」에서 공인인증서 또는 휴대폰 인증 후 희망일자를 선택하실 수 있습니다.

2020. 1. 17. 13:15, (알 수 없음) : The training procedure in federated learning is usually divided into four steps: client sampling, model broadcast (from the server to clients), local updates, and model aggregation (from clients to the server). Here, I propose that the data filtering algorithm and client filtering algorithm are inserted in the local updates step and model aggregation step, respectively, for developing a global single model.
Before explaining the aim, two terms should be clarified: private data and private cli-ent. Private data is the data which can leak the information a client and private client is the client who has a large percentage of private data. Then, the proposed algorithm follows below steps:
Step 1. Client sampling
Step 2. Model broadcast (from the server to clients)
Step 3. Data filtering & Local updates
Step 4. Client filtering & Model aggregation

In step 3, data filtering aims to divide the dataset at a client into general data and pri-vate data, and then local updates happen over the general data. In step 4, client filtering algo-rithm aims to divide the sampled clients at the server into general clients and private clients, and then server aggregates the general clients’ models. In summary, private data and clients do not used.
2020. 1. 17. 13:15, (알 수 없음) : The intuitions behind the proposed algorithm can be summarized:
1.	Not using private data and clients can help generalization.
2.	A client has general data and private data, but general data accounts for more than private data in general.
3.	Nevertheless, a small portion of clients tend to be the opposite.

2020. 1. 17. 13:39, (알 수 없음) : 1. private data / clients 안 사용 하는 게 좋을 걸?
2. private data는 local model을 specific하게 만드니까 빼는게 좋을 듯 (data filter의 직관) / 그럼에도 불구하고 general data가 일반적으로 많으니까 ㄱㅊ (data filter가 가능한 이유)
3. 그럼에도 user 자체가 private한 애가 있는데 얘도 뺴는게 좋을걸 (user filter의 직관) / 그럼에도 불구하고 general client가 일반적으로 많으니까 ㄱㅊ (user filter가 가능한 이유)
2020. 1. 17. 13:39, (알 수 없음) : 이거인데
2020. 1. 17. 13:41, 정우 : 1. private data를 사용하는 것이 generalization에 도움이 된다.
2. data는 두 종류가 있고, private이 아닌 애들은 general이라고 한다.
3. 일반적으로, general가 private보다 많은 비율을 차지한다.
4. 그니까 private은 빼도 된다.

2020. 1. 17. 17:38, (알 수 없음) : Fairness is a topic that gained attention in recent years, since it is important for AI systems and applications to not discriminate based on gender or race. For instance, if two people with all the same abilities but different gender or race are expected to earn different salaries, it is unfair. Actually, gender or race is one example of many factors related to fair-ness and factors depend on domain. If a task is changed to predict height in the previous ex-ample, gender or race becomes an important factor.

2020. 1. 17. 17:51, (알 수 없음) : Fairness is a topic that gained attention in recent years, since it is important for AI systems and applications to not discriminate based on particular characteristics. For in-stance, if two people with all the same abilities but different gender or race are expected to earn different salaries, it is unfair. However, if a task is changed to predict height in the previ-ous example, gender or race becomes an important factor. In summary, fairness is closely related to real-world sensitive domains and the definition of it can be varied ([41]).
